Structure desc      : top-level additive combination, contains transcendental functions log/cos, contains powers, 3 additive terms, complex structure (depth 6)
Fitted params       : c0=-1.2258e+00, c1=3.4033e-01, c2=-1.5708e+00, c3=-1.2258e+00, c4=-8.2606e-01, c5=-4.1303e-01, c6=1.0000e+00
Train NMSE          : 1.61e-13
Test NMSE           : 1.54e-13
OOD Test NMSE       : 1.05e-12

GT Equivalence Verification (PO26)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*log(Abs(v) + c0) - c1*beta*v - omega0**c2*x**c3
Candidate formulas: 86

GT (fixed):
\[
-2.45151654379511\,x^3\;+\;0.340325443007139\,\sin t\;-\;0.826056547542989\,v\;-\;0.413028273771494\,\log(|v|+1)
\]
So any matching candidate must be reducible (by choosing its free constants) to exactly: one \(x^3\) term, one linear \(v\) term, one \(\log(|v|+1)\) term, and one pure sinusoid in \(t\) (no extra \(t\)-dependence, no extra \(x\)/\(v\) couplings, no extra constants unless set to 0). Also \(\cos(t+\phi)\) can match \(\sin t\) via phase shift: \(\cos(t+\phi)=\sin t\) when \(\phi=-\pi/2\) (mod \(2\pi\)), with amplitude adjusted.

Below, “match” means we can set extra terms’ coefficients to 0 and tune remaining parameters to the GT coefficients and phase.

---

### 1. \(c0 x^3 + c1\cos(c2+t)+c3 x^3 + c4 v + c5\log(c6|v|+1)\)
- Combine \(x^3\): \((c0+c3)x^3\) can match \(-2.4515 x^3\).
- \(\cos(c2+t)\) can match \(+\sin t\) by choosing \(c2=-\pi/2\) and \(c1=0.3403254\).
- Linear \(v\): set \(c4=-0.8260565\).
- Log: need \(\log(|v|+1)\). Set \(c6=1\), \(c5=-0.4130283\).
All terms align; no leftovers. **Matches.**

### 2. \(c0 x^3 + c1\cos(c2+t)+c3 v + c4\log(c5|v|+1)\)
Same structure as GT (one \(x^3\), one trig-in-\(t\), one \(v\), one \(\log(|v|+1)\)).
Choose:
- \(c0=-2.4515165\)
- \(c1=0.3403254,\; c2=-\pi/2\)
- \(c3=-0.8260565\)
- \(c4=-0.4130283,\; c5=1\)
**Matches.**

### 3. \(c0 x^3 + c1\cos(c2+t)+c3 v + c4 v + c5\log(c6|v|+1)\)
- Linear \(v\) combines: \((c3+c4)v\) can match \(-0.8260565 v\).
- Others as in (1). Set \(c6=1\), tune trig phase, etc.
**Matches.**

### 4. Candidate 2 plus \(c6\,t/(c7 x+c8)+c9/(c7 x+c8)\)
Those rational terms depend on \(x\) (and \(t\) in numerator) and are not in GT. Only way to remove globally is set \(c6=0\) and \(c9=0\) (denominator choices can’t make them identically zero for all \(x,t\)). Then it reduces to candidate 2, which matches. **Matches.**

### 5. Includes \(c3 v x^2\) and extra \(c7 v\)
- \(v x^2\) term is not in GT; must set \(c3=0\).
- Then linear \(v\) becomes \((c4+c7)v\) which can match.
- Remaining terms match as before with phase/log tuning.
**Matches.**

### 6. Candidate 2 plus \(c6 v x^2\)
Set \(c6=0\) to remove coupling; remainder is candidate 2. **Matches.**

### 7. Candidate 2 plus \(c6\,t/(c7 v+c8)+c9/(c7 v+c8)\)
These are non-GT nonlinear functions of \(v\) and \(t\). Only removable by \(c6=0,c9=0\). Then reduces to candidate 2. **Matches.**

### 8. Candidate 2 plus \(c6 x (c7+t)^{c8}\)
Extra \(x\)-\(t\) coupling; set \(c6=0\). Reduces to candidate 2. **Matches.**

### 9. \(c0 x^3 + c1\cos(c2+t)+c3 x + c4 x^3 + c5 v + c6\log(c7|v|+1)\)
Extra linear \(x\) term not in GT ⇒ set \(c3=0\). Combine \(x^3\): \((c0+c4)x^3\) match. Others match with \(c7=1\), phase shift. **Matches.**

### 10. Candidate 2 plus \(c6 x/(c7 v+c8)+c9/(c7 v+c8)\)
Non-GT rational dependence on \(v\); set \(c6=0,c9=0\). Reduces to candidate 2. **Matches.**

### 11. Candidate 2 plus \(c6 v\cos(c7+c8 t)\)
Extra \(v\)-dependent oscillatory term; must set \(c6=0\). Then candidate 2. **Matches.**

### 12. Has \(c4\log(c5 x+1)\) plus \(c6\log(c7|v|+1)\)
GT has no \(\log(\text{affine in }x)\) term ⇒ set \(c4=0\). Then remaining is candidate 2 form (with log in \(|v|\)). **Matches.**

### 13. Two trig terms: \(c1\cos(c2+t)+c3\sin(c4 t+c5)\) plus \(v\) and log
GT needs only one sinusoid in \(t\). We can set one trig coefficient to 0 (e.g., \(c3=0\)) and use the other with phase shift to match \(\sin t\). Then tune \(x^3,v,\log\) as usual (set log scale to 1). **Matches.**

### 14. Candidate 2 plus extra \(c6\cos(c7+c8 t)\)
Extra independent trig term; set \(c6=0\). Then candidate 2. **Matches.**

### 15. Candidate 2 plus \(c6 \frac{v}{c7 v+c8}+ \frac{c9}{c7 v+c8}\)
Nonlinear rational-in-\(v\) terms; set \(c6=0,c9=0\). Then candidate 2. **Matches.**

### 16. Candidate 2 plus \(c6 \frac{v}{c7 x+c8}+ \frac{c9}{c7 x+c8}\)
Non-GT rational-in-\(x\) terms; set \(c6=0,c9=0\). Then candidate 2. **Matches.**

### 17. Has extra constant \(c1\) and extra \(c7 e^{c8 x}\cos(c9+t)\)
Set \(c1=0\) and \(c7=0\) to remove them. Remaining is \(x^3+\cos(t+\cdot)+v+\log(|v|+1)\) which can match. **Matches.**

### 18. Has extra constant \(c1\) and extra \(c4 x^{c5}\)
Set \(c1=0\). To avoid an extra non-\(x^3\) power term, set \(c4=0\) (or force it to merge with \(x^3\) by \(c5=3\); either works). Then match remaining terms. **Matches.**

### 19. Has extra constant \(c1\) and extra \(c7 x^5\)
Set \(c1=0\), \(c7=0\). Remaining matches candidate 22 form (see below). **Matches.**

### 20. \(c0 x^3 + (c1+c5)v + c2 + c3\cos(c4+t) + c6\log(c7|v|+1)\)
GT has no constant offset ⇒ set \(c2=0\). Then tune:
- \(c0=-2.4515\)
- \(c3\cos(c4+t)\) phase-shift to \(\sin t\)
- \(c1+c5=-0.8260565\)
- \(c6=-0.4130283,\;c7=1\)
**Matches.**

### 21. \(c0 x^{c1} + c2 + c3\cos(c4+t) + c5 v + c6 x^{c7}\log(c8|v|+1)\)
Problem: GT has a *pure* \(\log(|v|+1)\) term, not multiplied by \(x^{c7}\).
- If set \(c6=0\), we lose the log term entirely (can’t match GT).
- If keep \(c6\neq 0\), must make \(x^{c7}\equiv 1\) for all \(x\), i.e. \(c7=0\). Then log term becomes \(c6\log(c8|v|+1)\), OK with \(c8=1\).
Also need no constant: set \(c2=0\). And set \(c1=3\) to get \(x^3\).
Then tune coefficients/phases. **Matches.**

### 22. \(c0 x^3 + c1 + c2\cos(c3+t) + c4 v + c5\log(c6|v|+1)\)
Set \(c1=0\). Then tune \(c0,c2,c3,c4,c5,c6\) (with \(c6=1\) and phase shift) to match. **Matches.**

### 23. Candidate 2 plus \(c6 v (c7+t)^{c8}\)
Extra \(v\)-\(t\) coupling; set \(c6=0\). Then candidate 2. **Matches.**

### 24. Has \(c2 v x^2\) and extra \(c8 v\) and constant \(c1\)
Set \(c2=0\), \(c1=0\). Linear \(v\) combines \((c5+c8)v\) to match. Others match with phase/log tuning. **Matches.**

### 25. Candidate 2 plus \(c6 t/(c7 t+c8)+c9/(c7 t+c8)\)
These are non-GT functions of \(t\); set \(c6=0,c9=0\). Then candidate 2. **Matches.**

### 26. Has extra rational-in-\(x\): \(c4 x/(c5 x+c6)+c9/(c5 x+c6)\)
Set \(c4=0,c9=0\). Remaining is \(x^3+\cos(t+\cdot)+\log(|v|+1)+v\) which matches. **Matches.**

### 27. Includes \(c1|v|\) and \(c6 x^{c7}\log(\cdot)\)
GT has no \(|v|\) term ⇒ set \(c1=0\).
For the log term, same issue as candidate 21: need \(x^{c7}\equiv 1\) so set \(c7=0\) (and keep \(c6\neq 0\)), plus \(c8=1\).
Also remove constant \(c2=0\). Then tune remaining to match. **Matches.**

### 28. Has piecewise Max terms in \(v\): \(c2\max(0,-v)+c8\max(0,v)\)
GT is smooth linear in \(v\) (plus \(\log(|v|+1)\)). To avoid piecewise behavior, set \(c2=0,c8=0\). Also set constant \(c1=0\). Remaining matches candidate 22 form. **Matches.**

### 29. Has \(c4\log(c5 v+1)\) (no Abs) plus \(c7\log(c8|v|+1)\)
\(\log(c5 v+1)\) is not globally equivalent to \(\log(|v|+1)\) on sign-changing \(v\), and also has domain issues for negative \(v\). Must set \(c4=0\). Then tune the \(\log(|v|+1)\) term with \(c8=1\), and set constant \(c1=0\). **Matches.**

### 30. Has extra \(c4 e^{c5 v}\)
GT has no exponential in \(v\); set \(c4=0\). Set constant \(c1=0\). Remaining matches. **Matches.**

### 31. Has \(\sin(c6\log(c7|v|+1)+c8)\) instead of linear log term
A sine of a log cannot equal a linear log term for all \(v\) unless coefficient \(c5=0\) (removing it), but then we lose the required log term. No other log term present. **No match.**

### 32. Similar to 31: has \(\sin(\text{log}(\cdot))\) and no separate linear log term
Same obstruction: either keep sine(log) (nonlinear) or set it to 0 and lose log. **No match.**

### 33. Extra \(c6 e^{c7|x|}\sin(c8+c9 t)\)
Set \(c6=0\) to remove. Remaining is candidate 2. **Matches.**

### 34. Has \(c2 v^{c3}\) and \(c7 x^{c8}\log(\cdot)\) plus constant
Set constant \(c1=0\). Need linear \(v\): easiest set \(c2=0\) and use \(c6 v\) as linear term.
Need pure log: set \(c8=0\) so \(x^{c8}=1\), keep \(c7\neq 0\), set \(c9=1\).
Then tune \(x^3\) and trig phase. **Matches.**

### 35. Extra \(c7 v^3\)
Set constant \(c1=0\), set \(c7=0\). Remaining matches. **Matches.**

### 36. Has \(c4 v^{c5}\) plus linear \(c6 v\)
Set constant \(c1=0\). To avoid extra nonlinear \(v^{c5}\), set \(c4=0\). Then match with \(c6 v\) and log. **Matches.**

### 37. Has extra \(c4 e^{c5 v}\)
